 When and how did Rooh Afza enter the market and how is it disappearing? Where did Rooh Afza become for the first time? Rooh Afza, a Hakim Hafiz Abdul Majeed of Unani Herbal Medicine, invented exactly 113 years ago in Ghaziabad
 saal tha 1906
 In the same year, he opened a clinic called Hamdard in Lal Kuan Bazar, Old Delhi
 1907 main dilli main bheeshan garmi or lu se kaaphi log biimaar padane lage
 Then Hakim Abdul Majeed started giving the same dose of spirit to the patients
 lu or garmi se bachaane main hamdard kaa ruh afja kamaal kaa sabit hua

 ruh afja sirf dawa na hokar logon ko garmi se raahat dene kaa nayab nuskhaa ban gaya or hamdard dawaakhaana se badi company ban gai
 Rooh Afza became very famous among Muslim families, because during Ramadan, the daily drinkers used to drink this cold drink during Iftari

 abdul hamid or mohammad said

 1920 main hamdard dawaakhaana naam kii company kaa gathan hua
 Abdul Majeed had passed away

 Mohammad Saeed fled to Pakistan
 unhone karachi main hamdard kii shuruyaat kii

 Whereas elder son Abdul Hameed stayed in India with his mother
 abdul hamid ke do bete hue abdul moid or hammaad ahamed hue
 In 1948, the Hamdard company was made Waqf or Charitable and Mutavalli, Managing Director Abdul Moeed was created, while Hammad Ahmad took over marketing
 1948 kii vakf dead thi, lekin 1973 main ek sanshodhan kar diya or bade bete abdul moid ko chif mutavalli bana diya, jo vakf kaa finance, acount, production sab kuch dekhne lage

 is tarah board main abdul moid kii entry ho gai

 isi kaaran ruh afja kaa production nahin ho paa rahaa he

 There has been an increase in incidents of kidnapping for love here
 aankadon par gaur karen to rajya main pratidin pyaar paane ke liye kiye jane vaale apharan ke nau se zyada maamle darj kiye ja rahe hai
 a senior police officer in Bihar believes that initially, the girls' families link the incident of kidnapping and register a case of abduction of the girl, but after investigation, the matter turns out to be a love affair
 aise main police ko bhi kai pareshaani kaa saamana karnaa padataa he
 Significantly, other types of kidnapping incidents have come down in Bihar, while the increase in kidnapping incidents for love has been recorded
 agar sabhi tarah ke apharan kii ghatnaon ko jod diya jaae to apharan main prem conection ke aankaden sabhi par baari pad rahe hai
 According to the data recorded at the police headquarters, in the year 2012, 405 incidents of running away or kidnapping in the affair of Ishq have been recorded
 isamen sabase zyada june maheene main 50 maamle vibhinn thanon main darj kiye gaye hai
 According to police officials, out of these 405 incidents, only three incidents have gone wrong after research
 aankadon ke mutabik puure bihar main pichley varsh hatya ke liye apharan ke 278 maamle darj kiye gaye he, jabaki paise vasuuli ke liye maatr 86 maamle vibhinn thanon main darj kiye gaye hai
 Apart from the love connection in Bihar, there has also been an unprecedented increase in kidnapping incidents for marriage
 varsh 2012 main vivaah ke liye apharan kii 3007 ghatnaayen vibhinn thanon main darj kii gai hai, jisamen jaanch ke baad 15 maamle galat sabit hue
 If both the cases are combined then a total of 3412 cases of love connection and kidnapping for marriage have been registered in Bihar last year
 police adhikari bhi maanate hai ki aisi ghatnaayen police ke liye musiibat ban gai hai
 They say that in such incidents there is also a fear that the lover-girlfriend might fall into the wrong hands
